<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kloek.html>kloek</a> (64408)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cloec</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*cluoc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klōkaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloek.html>kloek</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloek.html>kloeker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">kloekst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>large, <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>stout</a></li>
<li>healthy, being in good health</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clever, wise</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kloekmoedig</span></li></ul>

<p>Onomatopoeic. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cluck</i>.

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clocke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klokka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">clocc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*klokkos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately of onomatopoeic origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klok.html>klok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>klokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokje.html>klokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uurwerk.html>uurwerk</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (wrist-)watch
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horloge.html>horloge</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>bell</li>
<li>protective <a href = vnd.unilang:cloche.html>cloche</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something bell-shaped, as some flowers</li></ol>

***klokhuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klokhuis.html>klokhuis</a> (82131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clochuus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bell tower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klok.html>klok</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house, casing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokhuis.html>klokhuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokhuizen.html>klokhuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokhuis.html>klokhuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The core (central part) of some fruit, containing the kernels or seeds</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">originally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A construction (building or part) which <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a> (a) bell(s) and/or where they are rung or cast (made)</li>
<li>Other <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> resembling the above by shape</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokkenluider.html>klokkenluider</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">klokvorm</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boothuis.html>boothuis</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">sterfhuis</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">eenhuizig</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:klokhuis.html>klokhuis</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

***klomp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klomp.html>klomp</a> (25298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clompe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump or mass of metal, wooden shoe, clump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klumpo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klumpô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump, clump, mass; clasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*glembʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clamp, mass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">klumpa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clump</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:klump.html>Klump</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Klumpen</i>. Related to <span class="Latn" lang="en">clamp</span>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg/250px-SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="199" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg/375px-SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg/500px-SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1914" data-file-height="1522" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:souvenir.html>Souvenir</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:klompjes.html>klompjes</a></b></i><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:souvenir.html>Souvenir</a> <b>clogs</b></div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klomp.html>klomp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klompen.html>klompen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klompje.html>klompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wooden shoe, clog.</li>
<li>A mass, a nugget, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">lump</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">chunk</span>.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clôyen</i> (variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clouwen</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*clōien</i>  (variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*clouen</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klawjaną</i>; possibly related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klooi.html>klooi</a></i> and a doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klauwen.html>klauwen</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clôot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klautaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cleat</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopjacht.html>klopjacht</a> (18983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klop.html>klop</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jacht.html>jacht</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klopjacht.html>klopjacht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klopjacht.html>klopjachten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klopjacht.html>klopjachtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">originally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> battue, hunting for game</li>

***klopje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopje.html>klopje</a> (38119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain, perhaps in reference to Christ who knocked (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:kloppen.html>kloppen</a></i>) at the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> of a woman's heart.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klopje.html>klopje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klopje.html>klopjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unmarried woman who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> dedicated her life to service to the Church.</li></ol>

***kloppen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kloppen.html>kloppen</a> (2495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cloppen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*cloppōn</i>, probably onomatopoeic. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">klopfen</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloppen.html>kloppen</a></i>.
</p>

***klos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klos.html>klos</a> (10407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">closse</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klos.html>klos</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klos.html>klossen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klosje.html>klosje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:spool.html>spool</a>, bobbin</li>
<li>wooden or metal reel or similar object</li>
<li>hardwood beam for sewing into planks, notably oak</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> testicle</li>
<li>klutz, clumsy person</li>
<li>target, victim (of a problem or joke)</li>
<li>lump, clod</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:cocoon.html>cocoon</a>,<a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></li>
<li>corn cob</li>
<li>fir-cone</li>
<li>horse's (lower) <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>; protuberance thereupon</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:spool.html>spool</a>, bobbin</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spoel.html>spoel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bobbijn</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">testicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>kloot</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teelbal.html>teelbal</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:testikel.html>testikel</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">klutz</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klungelen.html>klungel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">knoeier</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lomperd.html>lomperd</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lomperik</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An onomatopoeia.
</p>

***klucht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a> (23790)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluft</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clucht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kluft</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kluftiz</i> (whence also German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kluft</i>, English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cleft</i>). The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klieven.html>klieven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and the Middle Dutch meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> at first "separation, department", <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> also "neighbourhood of a town". The sense shifted to its modern meaning only in early modern Dutch times, starting with "nonsense, prattle" and then "joke, humorous story".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluchten.html>kluchten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>kluchtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a> play, farce</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">esp. Brabantian, figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chaotic, loud and/or ridiculous situation
<dl><dd><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a>, 'k <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlug.html>vlug</a> afgetrapt!"</i></dd>
<dd>'<i>Twas such a mess <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> there, I left as soon as I could!</i></dd>
<dd><i>"Da's <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijf.html>bedrijf</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b>!"</i></dd>
<dd><i>That company <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sooo mismanaged, hilarious!</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:letterkunde.html>letterkunde</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:meestal.html>meestal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kort.html>kort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toneelstuk.html>toneelstuk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarvan.html>waarvan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> plot <a href = vnd.unilang:komisch.html>komisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koe.html>koe</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschreven.html>geschreven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> Bredero.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li>lachwekkend <a href = vnd.unilang:voorval.html>voorval</a>

***kluis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluis.html>kluis</a> (1785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clūsa</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clausa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluis.html>kluis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluizen.html>kluizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluisje.html>kluisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A safe.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cashbox.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A locker.</li>
<li>A hermit's cell.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>hermitage</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">safe</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandkast.html>brandkast</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">locker</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">locker</span></li>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluisteren.html>kluister</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a fetter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">claudō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">close, shut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluit.html>kluit</a> (42075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cloud</i>. Related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>kloot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball; testicle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klont.html>klont</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluit.html>kluit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluiten.html>kluiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluitje.html>kluitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lump, clod (mostly in connection to earth or soil)

***kluiven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluiven.html>kluiven</a> (74929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klūvon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klūbōną</i>. Originally a weak verb, it became strong by analogy with other verbs.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluiven.html>kluiven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to gnaw, to nibble</li>
<li>to bite (a piece of meat) into <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> chunks</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluwen.html>kluwen</a> (64397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluwen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kliuwīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kliuwīną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klewô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*glew-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clew</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knagen.html>knagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gnaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps through  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nagetier</i>, eventually after  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rodens</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knaak.html>knaak</a> (104253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knaak.html>knaak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knaken.html>knaken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knaak.html>knaakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A 2½ guilders coin.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rijksdaalder</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large, valuable coin.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:knaak.html>knaak</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(numismatiek)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oud.html>oud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muntstuk.html>muntstuk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> ƒ2.50

***knaap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knaap.html>knaap</a> (5232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnāpe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cnapo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knappô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boy, youth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gnebʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, tighten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knappe.html>Knappe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knabe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knave</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">knape</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">knabe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">knapi</i>.
</p>

***knabbelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knabbelen.html>knabbelen</a> (24166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">knabbern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nibble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Both could ultimately be from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gnet-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, or imitative.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a> (39335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i>, whose sense “pretty” also occurs in old German attestations and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thought to be derived from “tight” <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> “tightly fitting” (of a piece of clothing). Further origin unsettled.  Also compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">næppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hardly at all</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knapper.html>knapper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am knappsten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scarce</li>
<li>lean <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having little <a href = vnd.unilang:extra.html>extra</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>somewhat less (than)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">ein <b>knappes</b> Jahr</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">a little less than a year</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> short or tight</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="de">Knappheit</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>narrowly; just
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Wir <a href = vnd.unilang:sind.html>sind</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></b> pünktlich.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>’re <b>just</b> in time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">knekel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
